info:Deluxe Room (2 beds)

info:6 Reviews

posted:Posted April 6, 2024
msg:I took my child to Dragon Nest and stayed here. The exterior and interior decoration are very beautiful, the price is affordable, and the waiters are very enthusiastic. After staying for one night, I will talk about the advantages and disadvantages of this hotel.
Advantages: It is a new hotel, clean and tidy, with complete facilities, a refrigerator, and a bathtub for children to take a bath. The breakfast is varied and tastes good. The child stayed for one night and said that he hopes to stay in this hotel often. It is a 10-minute walk from Xinghuo Station on Metro Line 3. There is a large shopping mall after getting off Xinghuo Station (you can buy snacks and drinks in this mall in advance if you go to Dragon Nest). The taxi fare from the hotel to Dragon Nest is 22 yuan.
Disadvantages: Non-intelligent control, the panoramic glass on the road side has poor sound insulation, and the sound of every car passing by rubbing against the road can be heard. There is a gap under the door, and the sound insulation is even worse. The footsteps, the door opening and closing, and the voices of the opposite door are very clear. It is recommended that the hotel can install sound insulation *****s under the door.

I like its independent bathroom and super large cloakroom the most. The cloakroom is an independent space with a hanging iron, a chair for changing clothes, and a shoe horn and shoe brush. You can take a bath in the bathtub while watching the scenery outside the window, with mountains and trains passing slowly, like a movie.
Disadvantages: There seems to be a problem with the drainage in the room I stayed in. Water ran out of it when I took a shower, and the entire bathroom floor was covered with water. The central air conditioner only had heating but no cooling at this time.
